Question #430 (ID: 705562)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: MB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
2:30 টার সময় ঘড়ির ঘণ্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণের পরিমাণ কত?

Options:
ক. 210° প্ৰায়
খ. 135° প্ৰায়
গ. 105° প্ৰায়
ঘ. 102° প্ৰায়


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
ঘণ্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার ঘর ব্যবধান [math]=\left\{30-\left(2 \times 5+5 \times \frac{30}{60}\right)\right\}=17 \frac{1}{2}[/math]
 ঘর[math]\therefore[/math]
 অন্তর্গত কোণ [math]\left(17 \frac{1}{2} \times 6^{\circ}\right)=105^{\circ}[/math]
বিকল্পঃ অন্তর্ভুক্ত কোণ [math]=\frac{1}{2}|60 \times \mathrm{H}-11 \times \mathrm{M}|=\frac{1}{2}|60 \times 2-11 \times 30|=105^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #439 (ID: 705549)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: DB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


উপরের চিত্রের জন্য -

(i) [math]AB^2=5[/math] একক

[math]\text { (ii) } 2 \cos \theta+\sqrt{3}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math] [math]\text { (iii) } \sin \theta+2 \cos ^{2} \theta=2[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:

[Image]
আবার, [math]sin \theta=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \theta=30^{\circ} \Rightarrow \theta=30^{\circ} \\\text { Option }(1): A C^{2}=A B^{2}+B C^{2} \\\Rightarrow(2)^{2}=A B^{2}+(1)^{2} \Rightarrow 4=A^{2}+1 \\\Rightarrow A B^{2}=3\\\text{Option (2): } 2 \cos \theta+\sqrt{3}=2 \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}+\sqrt{3}\\=2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\sqrt{3}=2 \sqrt{3}\\\text{Option (3): } \sin \theta+2 \cos ^{2} \theta\\=\sin 30^{\circ}+2\left(\cos 30^{\circ}\right)^{2}=\frac{1}{2}+2 \cdot\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{2} \\=\frac{1}{2}+2 \cdot \frac{3}{4}=\frac{1}{2}+\frac{3}{2}=\frac{1+3}{2}=2\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]cos(-300^{\circ})[/math]এর মান কত?

B. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos \left(-300^{\circ}\right)=\cos 300^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(3 \times 90^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)=\sin 30^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2}[/math]

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } \tan \theta=-\sqrt{3}\\\text{(ii) } \sin \theta=-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\\\text{(iii) } \cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

[math]\theta[/math]

[math]\text { [ }[/math]যেখানে [math]\left.0<\theta<\frac{\pi}{2}\right] \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. 0°
B. 30°
C. 60°
D. 90°


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{2}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \therefore \theta=48.2^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #475 (ID: 705526)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
2:16 টার সময় ঘড়ির ঘণ্টার কাঁটা ও মিনিটের কাঁটার অন্তর্গত কোণের পরিমাণ কত?

Options:
ক. 18°
খ. 26°
গ. 28°
ঘ. 30°


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
মিনিটের কাঁটার অবস্থান [math]=16[/math]
 ঘরে; ঘন্টার কাঁটার অবস্থান [math]=2 \times 5+16 \times \frac{1}{12}[/math]
 ঘরে [math]=\frac{34}{3}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 অন্তর্গত কোণ = ঘর ব্যবধান [math]\times 6^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(16-\frac{34}{3}\right) \times 6^{\circ}=\frac{14}{3} \times 6^{\circ} \equiv 28^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\tan \theta=\frac{3}{4}[/math] এবং [math]\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]cos \ theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]-\frac{5}{4}[/math]
B. [math]-\frac{4}{5}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{4}{5}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{5}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]-\frac{4}{5}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sec ^{2} \theta=1+\tan ^{2} \theta=1+\left(\frac{3}{4}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{25}{16} \Rightarrow \sec \theta=-\frac{5}{4}\left[\pi<\theta<\frac{3 \pi}{2}\right] \therefore \cos \theta=-\frac{4}{5}[/math]


Explanation:

ক. 9 কি.মি/ঘণ্টা (প্রায়)
খ. 27 কি.মি/ঘণ্টা (প্রায়)

3600 সেকেন্ডে অতিক্রম করে, [math]\frac{15.0796 \times 3600}{1000}[/math]
 কি.মি. [math]=54.287[/math]

Question:
[math]\frac{2 \pi}{11}=[/math]কত ?

Options:
A. 43°32'38"
B. 38°32'43"
C. 32°43'38.18"
D. 32°38'43.18"


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]Calculator[/math]
 অথবা [math]\frac{2 \times 180}{11}=32 \frac{8^{\circ}}{11}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} =32^{\circ}\left(\frac{8}{11} \times 60\right)^{\prime}=32^{\circ}\left(43 \frac{7}{11}\right)^{\prime} \\ =32^{\circ} 43^{\prime}\left(\frac{7}{11} \times 60\right)^{\prime}=32^{\circ} 43^{\prime} 38.18^{\circ} \end{array}[/math]

Question #496 (ID: 705505)

Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: MB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে পরবর্তী প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]AB=[/math] কত?

Options:
ক. [math]a^{2}-b^{2}[/math]
খ. [math]b^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
গ. [math]\sqrt{a^{2}-b^{2}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\sqrt{\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]\sqrt{\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]A B^{2}+a^{2}=b^{2} ; A B=\sqrt{b^{2}-a^{2}}[/math]

Explanation:

Question #505 (ID: 705487)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin ^{2} \theta=0[/math] হলে, [math]\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]2[/math]
B. [math]1[/math]
C. [math]\frac{1}{3}[/math]
D. [math]0[/math]


Correct Answer: D.[math]0[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} \theta=0 \therefore \sin \theta=0 \therefore \tan \theta=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{0}{1}=0[/math]


Explanation:

Question #506 (ID: 705488)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math] এবং [math]\cos A[/math] ও [math]\sin \mathrm{A}[/math] একই চিহ্নবিশিষ্ট হলে–

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } \sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\\\text{(ii) } \cot A=1\\\text{(iii) } \sec A+\tan A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
১ম চতুর্ভাগে [math]cos A[/math]
 ও [math]sin A[/math]
 এর একই [math]sign[/math]
 থাকে। [math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \therefore \mathrm{A}=45^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin A=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}, \cot A=1, \sec A+\tan A=\sqrt{2}+1[/math]


Explanation:

Question #507 (ID: 705489)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: SB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta+\sec \theta=p[/math] হলে, [math]\sin \theta[/math] এর মান নিচের কোনটি?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{2 p}{p^{2}+1}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{p^{2}-1}{p^{2}+1}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{p^{2}+1}{2 p}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{p^{2}+1}{p^{2}-1}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{p^{2}-1}{p^{2}+1}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin \theta}{\cos \theta}+\frac{1}{\cos \theta}=p \Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \theta}=p^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow \frac{(1+\sin \theta)^{2}}{1-\sin ^{2} \theta}=p^{2} \Rightarrow \frac{1+\sin \theta}{1-\sin \theta}=p^{2} \\ \Rightarrow \frac{2}{2 \sin \theta}=\frac{p^{2}+1}{p^{2}-1} \Rightarrow \sin \theta=\frac{p^{2}-1}{p^{2}+1} \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:


Sub-Questions:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan A=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\pi}{2}

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{(i) } A=\frac{5 \pi}{6}\\\text{(ii) } \sin ^{2} A=\frac{1}{4}\\\text{(iii) } \cos A=-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:
A. i,ii
B. i,iii
C. ii,iii
D. i,ii,iii


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \Rightarrow \tan \frac{5 \pi}{6} 8-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \Rightarrow \sin ^{2}\left(\frac{5 \pi}{6}\right)=\sin ^{2}\left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{6}=\frac{1}{4} \\ \Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{5 \pi}{6}\right)=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=-\cos \frac{\pi}{6}=-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \end{array}[/math]

Question #520 (ID: 705448)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: ChB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=-\frac{5}{12}[/math] এবং [math]\tan \theta, \sin \theta[/math] একই চিহ্নযুক্ত হলে, [math]\sec \theta[/math] এর মান [math]12[/math] কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{13}{5}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{13}{12}[/math]
C. [math]-\frac{13}{12}[/math]
D. [math]-\frac{13}{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta=-\frac{5}{12}[/math]
 এবং [math]\tan \theta \sin \theta[/math]
 উভয়েই ঋণাত্মক চিহ্নযুক্ত হওয়ায় [math]\theta[/math]
 এর অবস্থান চতুর্থ চতুর্ভাগে। চতুর্থ চতুর্ভাগে [math]sec\theta[/math]
ধনাত্মক।এখন, [math]\sec ^{2} \theta=1+\tan ^{2} \theta=1+\frac{25}{144}=\frac{169}{144} \therefore \sec \theta=\frac{13}{12}[/math]


Explanation:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]Cos2\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]0[/math]
B. 1/2
C. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
D. [math]1[/math]


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
যদি cos θ = √3/2 হয়, তাহলে θ = 30°। cos(2θ) এর মান নির্ণয় করার জন্য 2θ এর মান 60° হবে এবং cos(60°) = 1/2। সুতরাং, cos 2θ এর মান হলো 1/2।ধাপ:প্রথমে, cos θ = √3/2 থেকে θ এর মান বের করুন।আমরা জানি যে cos 30° = √3/2।অতএব, θ = 30°।এবার, cos 2θ এর মান নির্ণয় করুন।2θ = 2 * 30° = 60°।cos 2θ = cos 60°।আমরা জানি যে cos 60° = 1/2।সুতরাং, cos 2θ এর মান হলো 1/2।

Explanation:

Question:

B. [math]-\tan \theta[/math]

D. [math]-tan \theta[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\\=-\tan \left(\frac{13 \pi}{2}-\theta\right)=-\cot \theta[/math]

বাড়ি থেকে বিদ্যালয় পর্যন্ত পৌঁছাতে মিনিটের কাঁটাটির অগ্রভাগ কত দূরত্ব অতিক্রম করে?

Question #536 (ID: 705464)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\cot \left(\frac{n \pi}{4}+\theta\right)=1[/math] এবং [math]\theta=-\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হয় তবে [math]n[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. 1
B. 2
C. 3
D. 4


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cot \left(\frac{n \pi}{4}-\frac{\pi}{2}\right)=\cot \frac{\pi}{4} \Rightarrow \frac{n \pi}{4}-\frac{\pi}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{n \pi}{4}=\frac{3 \pi}{4} \therefore n=3[/math]


Explanation:

Question #537 (ID: 705465)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: MSB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]2 \sin ^{2} A+3 \sin A-2=0[/math] হলে, A = কত? যেখানে [math]0

Options:
A. [math]30°[/math]
B. [math]45°[/math]
C. [math]60°[/math]
D. [math]90°[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]30°[/math]

Solution:
[math]2 \sin ^{2} A+3 \sin A-2=0[/math]
বা, [math]2 \sin ^{2} A+4 \sin A-\sin A-2=0[/math]
বা, [math]2sinA (sinA +2)-1 (sinA + 2) = 0[/math]
বা, [math]2sinA-1) (sinA + 2) = 0[/math]
বা, [math], (sinA + 2) = 0[/math]
 অথবা, 2 [math]sinA -1 = 0 -1-0[/math]
বা, [math]sinA = - 2[/math]
 যা গ্রহণযোগ্য নয়বা, [math]\sin A=\frac{1}{2}=\sin 30^{\circ} \therefore A=30^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #540 (ID: 705468)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: RB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে পরবর্তী প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :

[math]sin \ A[/math] এবং [math]cos \ A[/math] বিপরীত চিহ্নবিশিষ্ট যেখানে $cos \ A = -13 $

[math]\operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{A}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
খ. [math]-\frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
গ. [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
ঘ. [math]\pm \frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\cos A=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \therefore \sin A=\sqrt{1-\left(-\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)^{2}}=\sqrt{1-\frac{1}{3}}=\sqrt{\frac{2}{3}} \\ \therefore \operatorname{cosec} A=\frac{1}{\sin A}=\sqrt{\frac{3}{2}} \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:

Question:
[math]\sin ^{2} \frac{2 \pi}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{3}=[/math] কত?

A. [math]\frac{5}{2}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]

D. [math]\frac{3}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]1[/math]

Solution:

 [math]\frac{\pi}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{3}=1[/math]

Question:
[math]\operatorname{cosec} A-\sin A=[/math]কত?

Options:
A. [math]\cos ^{2} A \cdot \operatorname{cosec} A[/math]
B. [math]\cos ^{2} A \cdot \sin A[/math]
C. [math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} A \cdot \cos A[/math]
D. [math]\operatorname{cosec}^{2} A \cdot \sec A[/math]


Correct Answer: A.[math]\cos ^{2} A \cdot \operatorname{cosec} A[/math]

Solution:
[math]\operatorname{cosec} A-\sin A=\frac{1}{\sin A}-\sin A[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\sin ^{2} A}{\sin A}=\cos ^{2} A \times \frac{1}{\sin A}=\cos ^{2} A \operatorname{cosec} A[/math]

Question #547 (ID: 705475)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: JB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sec \theta=-\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{2\pi}{3}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5\pi}{6}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{7\pi}{6}[/math]


Correct Answer: C.[math]\frac{5\pi}{6}[/math]

Solution:
[math]\sec \theta=-\frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 বা, [math]\cos \theta=-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \frac{\pi}{6}=\cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{6}\right)=\cos \frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=\frac{5 \pi}{6}[/math]


Explanation:

Question #549 (ID: 705477)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: MCQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: DiB
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=-1[/math] এবং [math]0<\theta<\pi[/math] [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:
A. [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
B. [math]\frac{3\pi}{4}[/math]
C. [math]\frac{5\pi}{4}[/math]
D. [math]\frac{7\pi}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: B.[math]\frac{3\pi}{4}[/math]

Solution:
[math]tan\theta=1[/math]
 বা, [math]\tan \theta=-\tan \frac{\pi}{4}=\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=\tan \frac{3 \pi}{4} \therefore \theta=\frac{3 \pi}{4}[/math]
